reaction_dwarf_civ

[OBJECT:REACTION]
	#notes: A- reactions in the individual race civ reaction files are for the
	# 'flavor' of the race.  reactions that are used in multiple races are not
	# 'flavor', and therefore are moved out of the reaction files for the races
	# and placed in individual files, so they appear as they really are a part
	# of a plug and play system of files for building the reactions of a race.
	# reactions will be here in the order as they appear in the entity file,
	# reactions that were removed to other files will have their file names 
	# listed.  Mods that are pulled out will be listed first as to keep these
	# remarks to a limited readable list.

###############################################################################
##### Vanilla building reactions ##############################################
	#A- if you can't find them here, they are in either:
	# reaction_vanilla.txt    - location of basic DF vanilla reactions
	# reaction_MW_vanilla.txt - location of MW reactions added to vanilla
	# reaction_smelter.txt    - location of all the smelting
	# reaction_embroidery.txt - mushroom dyes, mushroom cheese
	#
	#A- may remove mushroom dyes and mushroom cheese to a seperate file, why is
	# it in there? most likely due to it coming from one writer.

###############################################################################
##### Additonal PnP Mods (sets of buildings and/or reactions ##################
	# reaction_patron.txt       - reactions for patron buildings
	# reaction_liquids.txt      - Handpump and Waterweell reactions
	# reaction_silk.txt         - egg silk reactions, Kazoo
	# reaction_campfire.txt     - set fires from a campfire
	# reaction_archive.txt      - great archive building.
	# reaction_meph.txt         - Meph's decorations
	# reaction_trading.txt      - merchant shop reactions
	# reaction_pottery.txt      - all the clay/pottery reactions
	# reaction_steam_engine.txt - Steam enginge reactions
	# reaction_smelter.txt      - metallurgist is stored with the smelter
	# reaction_crematory.txt    - crematory reactions
	# reaction_library.txt      - library reactions
	# reaction_TESB.txt         - the earth strikes back mod reactions
	# reaction_modest_brew.txt  - all the modest mod reactions are found in
	# reaction_modest_mill.txt  - these three files.
	# reaction_modest_waterbarrel.txt
	# reaction_talior.txt       - tailor shop, expressed in other races.
	# reaction_inventor.txt     - inventor shop reactions.
	# reaction_embroidery.txt   - reactions for the dyer and embroidery studios.
    # reaction_mw_crafters.txt  - masterwork stone, wood, gem, bone crafters
	# reaction_poison_vat.txt   - poison vat reactions!
	# thatchery is currently inside of reaction_kobold...it will be moved.

##### Dwarf reactions - Dwarf flavor ##########################################

###############################################################################
#####  WEIGHT BENCH    ########################################################
	#A - even though its in humans also didn't feel it necessary to pull.
	# maybe a work out set, a mod file that holds all the work out rooms?
	# most of the other work out rooms are really flavor for those races, and
	# why humans have access is in itself an issue.  Its not their 'style'
[REACTION:WORK_OUT]
	[NAME:Work out - Lift boulders]
	[DESCRIPTION: Trains Strength, Agility, Toughness and Spatial/Kinetic attributes]
	[BUILDING:WEIGHT_BENCH:CUSTOM_A]
	[REAGENT:A:1:BOULDER:NONE:INORGANIC:NONE]
	[PRODUCT:100:1:BOULDER:NONE:GET_MATERIAL_FROM_REAGENT:A:NONE]
	[PRODUCT:100:1:BOULDER:NONE:INORGANIC:KNOWLEDGE_STONE]
	[PRODUCT:100:1:BOULDER:NONE:INORGANIC:KNOWLEDGE_STONE]
	[PRODUCT:100:1:BOULDER:NONE:INORGANIC:KNOWLEDGE_STONE]
	[PRODUCT:100:1:BOULDER:NONE:INORGANIC:KNOWLEDGE_STONE]
	[PRODUCT:100:1:BOULDER:NONE:INORGANIC:KNOWLEDGE_STONE]

###############################################################################
##### WOOD SPLITTING BLOCK    #################################################
	#A- why do dwarves get this? and humans get the stone splitter. personally
	# I hate this building, it doesn't produce enough material.  most wood
	# plank products use 2 planks or 1 wood, making this a minor chance for 
	# additional production, the human splitting stone produces 10 blocks.
[REACTION:SPLITTING_WOOD]
	[NAME:Split wood into planks]
	[BUILDING:WOOD_SPLITTING_BLOCK:CUSTOM_A]
	[REAGENT:A:1:WOOD:NONE:NONE:NONE]
	[PRODUCT:100:2:BLOCKS:NONE:GET_MATERIAL_FROM_REAGENT:A:NONE]
	[PRODUCT:50:1:BLOCKS:NONE:GET_MATERIAL_FROM_REAGENT:A:NONE]
	[SKILL:WOODCUTTING]

[REACTION:SPATTER_ADD_AMMO_ADAMANTINE]
	[NAME:Engrave adamantine runes (double damage)] 
	[BUILDING:RUNESMITH:CUSTOM_A]
	[DESCRIPTION:Causing the enemy to take double damage by any weapon on hit.]
	[DESCRIPTION:Uses Engraving skill.]
	[CATEGORY:AMMO_RUNE]
	[CATEGORY_NAME:Engrave ammo with runes]
	[CATEGORY_DESCRIPTION:Takes a stack of ammo and engraves it with powerful runes adding special effects to attacks. The effect depends on the metal used for the runes.]
	[CATEGORY_KEY:CUSTOM_A]
	[REAGENT:A:150:BAR:NONE:NONE:NONE]
		[REACTION_CLASS:ADAMANTINE_COATING]
	[REAGENT:object:5:AMMO:NONE:NONE:NONE]
		[PRESERVE_REAGENT]
	[IMPROVEMENT:800:object:COVERED:INORGANIC:ADAMANTINE_COATING]
	[SKILL:DETAILSTONE]
	[FUEL]
